<br> </font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:385;left:92 "><b>DRDGOLD RESPONDS TO DME
STATEMENT RE NORTH WEST OPERATIONS SEISMIC EVENT </b></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:400;left:352"><b>INQUIRY </b></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:415;left:668"> </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:430;left:90 "><font style="font-
size:11pt;line-height:20px;"><b>Johannesburg, South Africa. 17 October 2005</b>.
DRDGOLD Limited (JSE: DRD; <br>NASDAQ: DROOY; ASX: DRD; POM SoX: DRD)
  </font><font style="font-size:10.0pt;"> is aware of today&#8217;s media 
statement</font><font style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:18px;"><br>
  released by the Department of a Minerals and Energy relating to the inquiry 
into the seismic <br>event that occurred on 9 March at DRDGOLD&#8217;s North 
West Operations. <br> <br>DRDGOLD denies the correctness of the conclusions 
drawn by the Department from the <br>testimony presented at the inquiry. <br> 
<br>No evidence was presented to support the conclusion that there was: <br> 
</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:594;left:90 "><font style="font-
size:10.0pt;">&#8226;</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:595;left:96 "><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">
&nbsp; </font><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">  any shortage of support required
to make areas safe; </font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:611;left:90 "><font style="font-
size:10.0pt;">&#8226;</font><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">  &nbsp; 
</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:612;left:96 "><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">
&nbsp; </font><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">   inadequate ventilation; or 
</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:628;left:90 "><font style="font-
size:10.0pt;">&#8226;</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:629;left:96 "><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">
&nbsp; </font><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">   poor management control, as 
alleged. </font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:645;left:90 "><font style="font-
size:10.0pt;line-height:18px;"> <br>Although gullies were long, they were 
maintained as safely as far as reasonably practicable, <br>as required by law.  
<br> <br>There is, therefore, no basis for imposing any administrative fine on 
the owner of the mine. <br> <br>Furthermore, as far as the nature of the event 
is concerned, Dr Kijko, a seismologist with the <br>Council for Geoscience, 
testified that it was &#8220;very unlikely&#8221; that the event was caused by 
<br>active mining conducted by the mine or by regional mining in the area. <br> 
<br>DRDGOLD&#8217;s conclusion, therefore, is that the event was a natural 
earthquake. </font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:822;left:379"><b> </b></DIV>
<DIV style="position: absolute; top: 852; left: 90; width: 668; height: 
141"><font style="font-size:7pt;line-height:14px;"><b>Queries:</b>  <br> 
<br><b>South Africa</b>  <br>Investor and Media Relations  <br>Ilja Graulich, 
DRDGOLD  <br>+27 11 381 7826 (office)  <br>+27 83 604 0820 (mobile)  <br> 
<br>James Duncan, Russell &amp; Associates  <br>+27 11 880 3924 (office)  
<br>+27 82 892 8052 (mobile)  <br> <br> </font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:39;left:618"><font style="font-
size:11.0pt;"><b>Exhibit 99.1 </b></font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:60;left:70"><font style="font-size:7pt;"><b> 
</b></font></DIV>
</DIV>

<DIV style="position:absolute;top:277;left:668"> </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:287;left:90 "><font style="line-height:11px;">
<br>DRDGOLD is an intermediate unhedged gold producer with mines in South Africa
as well as Australasia. The company&#8217;s <br>production profile is split 
equally between its highly leveraged SA operations and its low cost, cash 
generative offshore <br>mines.  <br> <br>DRDGOLD has primary listings on the 
Johannesburg (JSE:DRD) and Australian (ASX:DRD) stock exchanges and 
<br>secondary listings on NASDAQ (DROOY), the London and Port Moresby stock 
exchanges and the Paris and Brussels <br>Bourses. Its shares are also traded on 
the regulated unofficial market of the Frankfurt Stock Exchange and the Berlin 
<br>OTC Market.  <br> <br>For more information, please visit www.drdgold.com  
</font></DIV>
